country_event = {
	id = 65001
	#trigger = {
	#	tag = OMG
	#	ai = yes
	#	not = { year = 1942 }
	#	not = { has_country_modifier = game_balance_tech_stage_1_cooldown }
	#}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	title = "HIDDEN TECHS"
	desc = "HIDDEN TECHS"
	picture = "blackice"
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		# game_balance_tech_stage_1a
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 0

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 1
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 1

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 2
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 2

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 3
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 3

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 4
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 4

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 5
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 5

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 6
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 6

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 7
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 7

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 8
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 8

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 9
						}
					}
				}
			}
			game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 4500
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "game_balance_tech_stage_1a_cooldown"
				duration = 118
			}
			#GER = { country_event = 650020 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "game_balance_tech_stage_1a_cooldown"
			duration = 118
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 65004
	#trigger = {
	#	tag = OMG
	#	ai = yes
	#	not = { year = 1942 }
	#	not = { has_country_modifier = game_balance_tech_stage_1b_cooldown }
	#}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	title = "HIDDEN TECHS"
	desc = "HIDDEN TECHS"
	picture = "blackice"
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		# game_balance_tech_stage_1b
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 0

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 1
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 1

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 2
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 2

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 3
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 3

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 4
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 4

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 5
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 5

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 6
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 6

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 7
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 7

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 8
						}
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 8

						not = {
							game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 9
						}
					}
				}
			}
			game_balance_tech_stage_1b = 4500
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "game_balance_tech_stage_1b_cooldown"
				duration = 118
			}
			#GER = { country_event = 650020 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "game_balance_tech_stage_1b_cooldown"
			duration = 118
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = 530010
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {

		not = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "GBP_experience"
				value = 150
			}
		}
		war = yes

		not = {
			grand_battle_plan = 1
			has_country_modifier = GBP_experience_CD
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			controller = {
				grand_battle_plan = 1
				war_with = THIS
			}
		}
		last_battle_loser_losses = 1000

		not = {
			last_battle_loser_losses = 2000
		}
	}
	title = "EVTNAME530013"
	desc = "EVTDESC530013"
	picture = "doctrine_learn"
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA530013"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		THIS = {
			any_controlled = {
				limit = {
					country_units_in_province = THIS
					units_in_province = 1
					any_neighbor_province  = {
						limit = {
							controller = {
								grand_battle_plan = 1
								war_with = THIS

								not = {
									blitzkrieg = 1
									superior_firepower = 1
									deep_battle_doctrine = 1
								}
							}
							units_in_province = 1
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = learn_grand_battle_plan_province_flag_2
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_I"
						duration = 1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "GBP_experience"
						value = +5
					}
				}
				25 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_II"
						duration = 1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "GBP_experience"
						value = +7
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			country_event = 530006
		}
		# TEST
	}

					units_in_province = 1
					any_neighbor_province  = {
						limit = {
							controller = {
								blitzkrieg = 1
								war_with = THIS

								not = {
									superior_firepower = 1
									deep_battle_doctrine = 1
									grand_battle_plan = 1
								}
							}
							units_in_province = 1
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = learn_blitzkrieg_province_flag_2
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_I"
						duration = 1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_CD"
						duration = 7
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "BK_experience"
						value = +5
					}
				}
				40 = {
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_II"
						duration = 1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_CD"
						duration = 7
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "BK_experience"
						value = +7
					}

					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_III"
						duration = 1
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "BK_experience_CD"
						duration = 7

					change_variable = {

			}
		}

			has_country_modifier = BK_experience_CD
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {

				blitzkrieg = 1
				war_with = THIS
			}
		}
		last_battle_winner_losses = 4500

country_event = {
	# LVL 1
	id = 969700
	trigger = {
		ENG = {
			check_variable = {
				which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG"
				value = 0.01
			}

			not = {
				check_variable = {
					which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG"
					value = 1.01
				}
			}
		}

		not = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II
		}
		has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	title = "Trade Deal Closed"
	desc = "Trade deal will last for one year. Over this period of time United Kingdom will supply us with constant stream of Chromite."
	picture = "chromium_trade"
	option = {
		name = "OK"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I"
			duration = 460
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

				which = "trade_resource_tungsten_JAP"
				value = 0.01
			}

country_event = {
	id = 969760
	trigger = {

		not = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG
		}
		or = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	title = "Trade Expired"
	desc = "Our trade deal for Chromite with United Kingdom has expired. We need to refresh it or find different source."
	picture = "chromium_trade_expired"
	option = {
		name = "Time to browse our options again."
		ENG = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG"
				value = -1
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II
	}
}

	trigger = {

		not = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_aluminium_HUN
		}
		or = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_aluminium_HUN_cooldown_I
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_aluminium_HUN_cooldown_II
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	title = "Trade Expired"
	desc = "Our trade deal for Aluminium with Hungary has expired. We need to refresh it or find different source."
	picture = "aluminium_trade_expired"
	option = {
		name = "Time to browse our options again."
		HUN = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "trade_resource_aluminium_HUN"
				value = -1
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_aluminium_HUN_cooldown_I
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_aluminium_HUN_cooldown_II
	}
}

################################
### PAY THAT GODDAMN RENT!!! ###

country_event = {
	#introduction
	id = 7900
	trigger = {
		ai = no

		not = {
			has_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start
		}
		or = {
			has_country_flag = BlackICE
			has_country_flag = Multiplayer
		}
	}
	title = "Budget limitations heads up"
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = "salary_events"
	option = {
		name = "Time to prepare our budget."
		set_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = 7961
	trigger = {
		ai = no

		not = {
			has_country_flag = budget_over_2000
		}
	}
	title = "Budget reserves"
	desc = "Our budget is settled. We are aware of our potential expenses and the amount of money we need to keep in reserve."
	picture = "salary_events"
	option = {
		name = "We need to be careful from now on."
		set_country_flag = budget_over_2000
	}
}
#######################
##### ARMY EVENTS #####
#######################
country_event = {
	#1st
	id = 7901
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		has_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start
		or = {
			has_country_flag = BlackICE
			has_country_flag = Multiplayer
		}
		or = {
			and = {
				or = {
					faction = axis
					tag = CHI
				}
				total_amount_of_brigades = 1000

				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 1100
				}
			}
			and = {
				faction = comintern
				total_amount_of_brigades = 1700

				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 1800
				}
			}
			and = {
				or = {
					faction = allies
					and = {

						not = {
							faction = allies
							faction = axis
							faction = comintern
							tag = CHI
						}
					}
				}
				total_amount_of_brigades = 700

				not = {
					total_amount_of_brigades = 800
				}
			}
		}

		not = {
			has_country_modifier = pay_soldiers_cooldown
		}
	}
	title = "Our Army asks for more money"
	desc = "EVTDESC7901"
	picture = "salary_events"
	option = {
		name = "OK - pay this time"
		money = -450
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_I"
			duration = 90
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_cooldown"
			duration = 90
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "NO - don't pay this time"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_I_NO"
			duration = 90
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_cooldown"
			duration = 90
		}
	}
}

			tag = USA
		}

			faction = this
		}

		not = {

		}

	}

	}

country_event = {
	id = 41306
	title = "TRAINING LAW start"
	desc = "Minimal to basic"
	picture = "doctrine_learn"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = "ELITE"
		OMG = {
			### LAND ###
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							minimal_training_land_tech = 1

							not = {
								has_country_flag = units_training_law_START
								training_laws = minimal_training
							}
							training_laws = basic_training
						}
						and = {
							has_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag

							not = {
								training_laws = minimal_training
							}
							training_laws = basic_training
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = units_training_law_START
				set_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag
				clr_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag
				minimal_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
				basic_training_land_tech = 25000
			}
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							minimal_training_land_tech = 1

							not = {

				set_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START
				set_country_flag = minimal_training_naval_tech_flag
				clr_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag
				specialist_training_naval_tech_revert = 25000
				minimal_training_naval_tech = 25000
			}
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							specialist_training_naval_tech = 1

							not = {
								has_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START
								naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval
							}
							naval_units_training_laws = basic_training_naval
						}
						and = {
							has_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag

							not = {
								naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval
							}
							naval_units_training_laws = basic_training_naval
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START
				set_country_flag = basic_training_naval_tech_flag
				clr_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag
				specialist_training_naval_tech_revert = 25000
				basic_training_naval_tech = 25000
			}
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							specialist_training_naval_tech = 1

							not = {
								has_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START
								naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval
							}
							naval_units_training_laws = advanced_training_naval
						}
						and = {
							has_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag

							not = {
								naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval
							}
							naval_units_training_laws = advanced_training_naval
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START
				set_country_flag = advanced_training_naval_tech_flag
				clr_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag
				specialist_training_naval_tech_revert = 25000
				advanced_training_naval_tech = 25000
			}
		}
	}
}
